  hello again dewdz kropka i hope you were            /______|
  fully satisfied after watching my twenty
  fifth  ascii  collection  kropka  here i
  am on the rush hours party 1997 and i am
  proud to  say myslnik i have done it now
                                wykrzyknik  as  always try to look  for some
                                attractions  and requested  logo stuff  down
                                here kropka this piece of azkee is dedicated
                                to all my friends around the world przecinek
                                which likes my puny art kropka i am not good
  in it but i want to take a toast kropka
  toast for  the amiga  przecinek  future
  przecinek  dear sceners  and  of course
  our  big  creative power  kropka  dewdz
  przecinek do your job good  as hell for
                                the future generations wykrzyknik last thing
                                i want to say is  a note for the founder/u'r
                                myslnik man przecinek new school is not suck
                                przecinek  it gives  you more  possibilities
                                of creating  your own  style kropka  try  to
  create something in n`skool  kropka  so
  przecinek  time to  go and take  a look
  into  my job kropka  man przecinek come
  to  polish  patirs because  only  poles
  knows przecinek how to spent party time

     cheers everyone for polish scene domination in nineteen ninetyseven
                  dave przecinek come back to us wykrzyknik

                   rush hours`97 and sdv6 special edition

       * musical inspiration: the chemical brothers, apollo 440, yello
         enya, the prodigy, jam & spoon, sven  vath, marusha and a lot
         of amiga modules (goa, hardtrance, ambient and classic style)

       * main art done by me in three weeks of hard work

       * i wanna say thanks to some pals which help me to create this
         puny design by their losos: the founder/u'race, spøk/link124
         sundance/doggystyle, dave/u'race, acid/doggystyle, qki/l124.
         all of you thanks again and still support me :)
